<div id="review_3113257012" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3113257012" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3113257012?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/43358884-sorcery-of-thorns">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3113257012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4259336762688743774"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579354414i/28799415._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Ink and parchment flowed through her veins. The magic of the Great Libraries lived in her very bones. They were a part of her, and she a part of them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I always thought booklice were a nuisance until I read this book, and Elisabeth made me wish I were one. Wouldn’t it be awesome to wield a power much like the one she possesses? This book is a much appreciated tribute to all book lovers in the world. But that’s exactly where the specialty ends. I see four and five star ratings everywh</span>
  <span id="freeText4259336762688743774" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579354414i/28799415._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Ink and parchment flowed through her veins. The magic of the Great Libraries lived in her very bones. They were a part of her, and she a part of them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I always thought booklice were a nuisance until I read this book, and Elisabeth made me wish I were one. Wouldn’t it be awesome to wield a power much like the one she possesses? This book is a much appreciated tribute to all book lovers in the world. But that’s exactly where the specialty ends. I see four and five star ratings everywhere, and I’m sad to say that I can’t relate to the experience.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508784473ra/24254146.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I drifted in and out of sleep while listening to the audiobook. The narration actually had a pretty great flow and was well animated. But the story failed to keep my attention. The pacing was a little slow and picked up after some filler scenes in the middle. When it was finally time for the big showdown, I was already too bored to care. If you were to ask me how it all went down, I honestly couldn’t be sure I’d be able to recount anything. Can someone please tell me what has become of Silas?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You belonged in the library, as much as any book.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The characters didn’t exist beyond their assigned roles. They also kinda felt like the cheap carbon copies of Will, Jem, and Tessa from <i>The Infernal Devices</i>. I enjoyed their banter immensely though. I liked Nathaniel and Silas mostly because their type of characters is always the most appealing and entertaining one to read. Otherwise, they were all just a group of two dimensional characters.<br><br><blockquote>
<b>Elisabeth</b>, the quiet bookworm who gets to save the world; <b>Nathaniel</b>, the tortured, good looking, and sarcastic male love interest who’s got a tragic past; <b>Silas</b>, the mysterious demon guy who’s secretly just a soft boi at heart; <b>Katrien</b>, the ever so helpful and always resourceful best friend; and <b>Ashcroft</b>, the bad guy with a hero complex.</blockquote><br>Plotwise, it was predicatable. Not exactly a bad thing, but definitely made me yawn and roll my eyes quite a number of times. The concept of this book was astonishing, and the world building was interesting. I felt for Elisabeth through her love for books. However, I was just not 100% sold on how the plot developed. It’s a shame really because the cover is so gorgeous. I don’t think I’ll ever read this author again considering I also didn’t like her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2180636357?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">debut</a> novel. I guess it couldn’t be helped that her books are not my cup of tea.<br><br><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4259336762688743774" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2855291544?book_show_action=true">Jun 12, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zainab" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zainab" href="/user/show/48759239-zainab">Zainab</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2855291544" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11706082408127146953">Since this is one of the most anticipated book of the year and not a lot of people have read it, I am going to keep this spoiler free.<br/><br/>The book started out great. We have our main character Elisabeth who is what most people would call 'innocent'. She isn't too smart- I mean <i>I</i> found her to be a bit too childish. Anyway, she's an orphan who works/lives in this Great Library and tries a bit too hard to impress her director.<br/>Then something happens and she gets kicked out of the library and so this is </span>
  <span id="freeText11706082408127146953" style="display:none">Since this is one of the most anticipated book of the year and not a lot of people have read it, I am going to keep this spoiler free.<br /><br />The book started out great. We have our main character Elisabeth who is what most people would call 'innocent'. She isn't too smart- I mean <i>I</i> found her to be a bit too childish. Anyway, she's an orphan who works/lives in this Great Library and tries a bit too hard to impress her director.<br />Then something happens and she gets kicked out of the library and so this is where the story starts when this 'charming' young sorcerer Nathaniel takes her somewhere along with his mysterious servant Silas of whom Elisabeth thinks of as 'remarkable' (don't ask me)<br /><br /><br /><b>The Good:</b><br />•Elisabeth's positivity.<br />•Nathaniel's back story.<br />•The mysteries (albeit predictable)<br /><br /><br /><b>The Bad:</b><br />•The dialogues- they were a bit too cheesy.<br />• The book is <i>dragged</i>. It could've easily been a 300 (or less) paged book.<br />•It was a bit too predictable.<br /><br />All in all, it's not a bad book just 'keep your expectations low' kinda book.</span>

<div id="review_2588465592" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2588465592" />
    <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader"><img alt="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579173421p2/43850323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2588465592?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader">Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=fantasy-books">fantasy-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-really-want-to-kiss-the-hero">i-really-want-to-kiss-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=romance-books">romance-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=stole-my-heart">stole-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=great-romance">great-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-want-to-live-in-this-world">i-want-to-live-in-this-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=slow-burn-romance">slow-burn-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=my-book-crushes">my-book-crushes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=so-funny-lol">so-funny-lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=ya-books">ya-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2588465592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7573265410682186109"><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>
<br/>"But there is always more than one way to see the world. Those who claim otherwise would have you dwell forever in the dark."<br/>
</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>Wow. I haven't been moved by a book since ... I don't know ... months ago probably. This book was breathtaking. It was incredibly beautiful and so different than what I have ever read. What a fresh breath of air! and I even bought another copy of this book for my friend's birthday present and I had given it to her yesterday and when her fa</span>
  <span id="freeText7573265410682186109" style="display:none"><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>
<br>"But there is always more than one way to see the world. Those who claim otherwise would have you dwell forever in the dark."<br>
</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Wow. I haven't been moved by a book since ... I don't know ... months ago probably. This book was breathtaking. It was incredibly beautiful and so different than what I have ever read. What a fresh breath of air! and I even bought another copy of this book for my friend's birthday present and I had given it to her yesterday and when her face lit up with delight and I felt my heart was bursting with happiness because she liked it that I gave her this book. I was just so enthralled by this book that I wanted my friend to also read it. YES, the book was <b>THAT</b> good<br><br>I laughed. I giggled. I grinned. I cursed. I cried. This book made me feel a lot of emotions. IT IS LITERALLY THE BEST FEELING when you read a book and even the quotations in this book were beautiful. Wow. Now, I'm going to tell you in detail what I loved from this book. <br><br><br><b>
  <u>The Plot</u>
</b><br><br>THE PLOT WAS SO GOOD *screams* It was so different that what I have ever read. So in this book there are grimoires. These are the books that can whisper, move and they can even transform into a monster, malefict, if they are provoked with a damage. SOUNDS SO AWESOME, doesn't it? and I would say that the pacing in this book was slow but not the kind of slow that made you want to throw the book. It was the perfect kind of slowness. It wasn't rushed and the book took time to explain things. I swear this book is such a fresh breath of air. The world in the book was so mesmerizing and I honestly don't know how many times I have whispered to myself that I wanted to live in the world of this book so bad. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1563648453ra/27861276.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admit I didn't love the book instantly from the start but I kept reading it because I don't know why this book was just so intriguing and I wanted to keep reading it and I eventually fell in love with the book and the characters. It was inevitable for me to not fall in love with this book when it was such an incredible book. <br><br><b>
  <u>The Characters</u>
</b><br><br>I LOVE THE CHARACTERS SO MUCH I wanted to cry. So firstly, I want to talk about Nathaniel. This guy ... where can I get a guy like him in my life? <b>Nathaniel</b> was just so cute, funny and such a fierce character. He made me squeal in delight and put my hand over my chest because he TOUCHED my cold heart. He made me laugh so many times and I don't laugh that often when I read so he made me laugh clearly said something here. Again, WHERE THE FUCK CAN I GET A GUY LIKE HIM? I would totally date a guy like him. ❤<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1563649001ra/27861290.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Elizabeth</b> was also the main character in this book and I ADORED her. She was such a fierce character, she did not give up easily when she had a problem and she honestly inspired me to not give up and to do my best to solve whatever problem I have in my life and on top of that Elizabeth was also a kind character. She is definitely on the list of the characters that have inspired me. If I could hug her to say my thanks, I would but I couldn't so I hug the book instead. Ms. Rogerson is such a brilliant author. <br><br><b>Silas</b> was also one of my characters in this book. I don't want to explain you about him in detail because I don't trust myself enough to not slip a minor spoiler, but I can tell you that he's such a complex character and I loved him so much. I wanted to hug him. Well, basically I wanted to give a hug or a lot of hugs to Elizabeth, Nathaniel and Silas. These characters were wonderful and they made the book more intriguing, more incredible and certainly more beautiful. I <s>loved</s> love these characters. <br><br><b>
  <u>The Romance</u>
</b><br><br>The romance was so beautiful and it completely stole my heart. I loved the interactions between Nathaniel and Elizabeth and the romance between them was so real and beautiful. They respected each other and loved each other. I want this kind of romance in my life ahhhh. The romance was definitely a slow burn romance. MY FAVORITE! but I do not really think it's an enemies-to-lovers kind of romance, I mean Elizabeth never hated Nathaniel but she wasn't exactly fond of him in the beginning. The development of their relationship was beautiful. JUST READ THE BOOK. IT IS SO GOOD. <br><br>the reason I didn't give it 5 stars was because for me 5 stars are for books that I will reread again and again. While I loved this book very much, I do not think I will reread it. But hey, we'll see whether I will ever reread this book or not because I absolutely loved this book. <br><br><b>Thank you so much for reading and liking this review. I appreciate it very much and I highly recommend you all to read this mesmerizing book. It is action-packed and it has incredible characters. This book is awesome! *clap hands* and I hope you all have an amazing weekend! </b>❤❤<br><br><br><br><br>•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><br><b>REVIEW TO COME SOON. <br><br>All I can say right now is that this book was wonderful and I had a lot of emotions reading it. I loved it and now I'm going to hug the book. Bye. <br></b><br><br>•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><br><br><s>
  <b><br>AT LAST, I AM FREE FROM READING SLUMP and even in a good timing in which my examinations are ended. WOO HOO! Lucky me! Moreover, this book has slow burn romance and I'm not even gonna lie that it's actually the first reason I'm reading this book. <br><br>Have you read it? Or do you plan to? <br></b>
</s></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2587023605" />
    <a title="Hamad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54464244-hamad"><img alt="Hamad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577880699p2/54464244.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2587023605?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hamad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hamad" href="/user/show/54464244-hamad">Hamad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=good-covers">good-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=2019-reads">2019-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=hardcovers">hardcovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2587023605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer558118568679560808"> <a href='https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/2019/09/30/sorcery-of-thorns-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>This Review</a> ✍️ <a href='https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Blog</a> 📖 <a href='https://twitter.com/Hamad9626' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> 🐦 <a href='https://www.instagram.com/thebookprescription/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> 📷<br/><br/> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Knowledge always has the potential to be dangerous. It is a more powerful weapon than any sword or spell.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>🌟 I do believe in second chances and I give every author 2 chances before deciding that their style is or isn’t for me. I did not like Margaret’s debut AEoR and I predicted that its rating will decrease upon its release and that really happened. It has an average rating of 3.66 now. But enough about that book because it was a standa</span>
  <span id="freeText558118568679560808" style="display:none"> <a href="https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/2019/09/30/sorcery-of-thorns-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">This Review</a> ✍️ <a href="https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> 📖 <a href="https://twitter.com/Hamad9626" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> 🐦 <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookprescription/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> 📷<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Knowledge always has the potential to be dangerous. It is a more powerful weapon than any sword or spell.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />🌟 I do believe in second chances and I give every author 2 chances before deciding that their style is or isn’t for me. I did not like Margaret’s debut AEoR and I predicted that its rating will decrease upon its release and that really happened. It has an average rating of 3.66 now. But enough about that book because it was a standalone and a debut and I could tell the author had more potential and turns out I am right!<br /><br />🌟 This one felt like a love letter to all the bookworms out there! It takes place in libraries and there are living books and bookworms and magic and everything that book fans will relate to. I think that was very smart of the author because this setting is one that all book fans will be comfortable with and like. She’s also smart because her covers were designed by Charlie Bowater, a very great artist whose art is getting more recognition every day!<br /><br />🌟 I am not going to keep mentioning AEoR, but I am going to say that this was much better. The writing, characters, world building and plot all were heaps better. The writing was much more dynamic in this one and not boring. There was a mix of beautiful prose and banter and seriousness.<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It was always wise to be polite to books, whether or not they could hear you.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />🌟 The characters were well written, Elizabeth was great and the whole library thing gave her Belle (from Beauty and the Beast )vibes, Nathaniel was interesting too and the romance was slow and made sense. The secondary characters were all well written too.<br /><br />🌟 The world was not very complicated for a fantasy book but it was intriguing. As I said above, who does not want to read about magical libraries and living books and grimoires and demons!<br /><br />🌟 The pacing was somewhere in the middle leaning more toward fast pacing, I do remember a lot of things happening. I think the book could have been a bit shorter because some parts were too stretched out and boring. But overall, I was enjoying it!<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“When terrible things have happened to you, sometimes the promise of something good can be just as frightening.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />🌟 Summary: This was definitely better than the author’s debut! If you did not like the first book then this is worth giving a chance. I think it is a bit over-hyped but still enjoyable. There was great improvement of the author’s writing abilities and that’s why I am generous with my rating! If the idea of a magical library sounds fancy for you, then I do recommend this one!<br /><br />You can get more books from <a href="https://www.bookdepository.com/?a_aid=2611996" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Depository</a><br /></span>

    <a title="megs_bookrack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack"><img alt="megs_bookrack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532027727p2/48328025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2591948034?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="megs_bookrack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="megs_bookrack" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack">megs_bookrack</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48328025-megs-bookrack?shelf=ya-fantasy-to-read">ya-fantasy-to-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48328025-megs-bookrack?shelf=books-i-own-to-read">books-i-own-to-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2591948034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14452772990880043785"><u>Synopsis:</u><br/> <br/><i>
  <b>...imaginative fantasy about an apprentice at a magical library...</b>
</i><br/><br/>I'm like...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1542042783ra/26583927.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Purchased.<br/><br/><u>Update:</u><br/><br/>Who am I that I have owned this since release day and haven't gotten to it yet?<br/><br/>Oh yeah, that's totally me.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1564508899ra/27913190.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></span>
  <span id="freeText14452772990880043785" style="display:none"><u>Synopsis:</u><br> <br><i>
  <b>...imaginative fantasy about an apprentice at a magical library...</b>
</i><br><br>I'm like...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1542042783ra/26583927.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Purchased.<br><br><u>Update:</u><br><br>Who am I that I have owned this since release day and haven't gotten to it yet?<br><br>Oh yeah, that's totally me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1564508899ra/27913190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14452772990880043785" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2570827799" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10543992133785569694">She has done it again!! I loved An Enchantment of Ravens, Margaret’s debut, so I was so excited to read this and it did not disappoint! This was such a wild ride - beautiful writing, an epic story and charming characters (I can’t decide who my favourite is).</span>

<div id="review_2833028277" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2833028277" />
    <a title="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens"><img alt="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597139554p2/59033840.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2833028277?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Althea | themoonwholistens ☾" href="/user/show/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens">Althea | themoonwholistens ☾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=highly-recommended">highly-recommended</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=favourite-standalones">favourite-standalones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=rep-lgbtq">rep-lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=favourites-of-all-time">favourites-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=genre-high-fantasy">genre-high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=made-me-cry-and-my-heart-ache">made-me-cry-and-my-heart-ache</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=best-audiobooks">best-audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=favourite-characters">favourite-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59033840-althea-themoonwholistens?shelf=read-audiobook">read-audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2833028277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3255568437145614407"><blockquote>
  <i>”There is always more than one way to see the world. Those who claim otherwise would have you dwell forever in the dark.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>FORMAT READ:</b> Audiobook (Recommended) & eBook <br/><b>SIMILAR VIBES:</b> The Infernal Devices, Daughter of a Burning City, A Curse So Dark and Lonely<br/><b>READ FOR:</b> broody banter, if you want to laugh and love<br/><b>READING LEVEL:</b> Level 2-3 out of 5<br/><br/>⟹ <a href='https://themoonwholistens.wixsite.com/mysite' rel='nofollow noopener'>MY BLOG</a> ⟸<br/>⟹ <a>SUPPORT ME ON KO-FI</a> ⟸<br/><i>*All of my reviews are as spoiler-free as possible unless states otherwise* </i><br/><br/><b>
  <u>OVERALL THOUGHTS:</u>
</b> 4.75<br/><br/>FUTURE ALTHEA UP</span>
  <span id="freeText3255568437145614407" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>”There is always more than one way to see the world. Those who claim otherwise would have you dwell forever in the dark.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>FORMAT READ:</b> Audiobook (Recommended) &amp; eBook <br><b>SIMILAR VIBES:</b> The Infernal Devices, Daughter of a Burning City, A Curse So Dark and Lonely<br><b>READ FOR:</b> broody banter, if you want to laugh and love<br><b>READING LEVEL:</b> Level 2-3 out of 5<br><br>⟹ <a href="https://themoonwholistens.wixsite.com/mysite" rel="nofollow noopener">MY BLOG</a> ⟸<br>⟹ <a>SUPPORT ME ON KO-FI</a> ⟸<br><i>*All of my reviews are as spoiler-free as possible unless states otherwise* </i><br><br><b>
  <u>OVERALL THOUGHTS:</u>
</b> 4.75<br><br>FUTURE ALTHEA UPDATE: I realized that this reminds me of The Infernal Devices... which is <i>probably</i> why I lost my mind reading it<br><br>HOLY HOLY OHMYGOSH THAT WAS SO GOOD<br><br>PERFECT. ENDING. PERFECT. EVERYTHING.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517636101ra/24993508.gif" width="250" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>me when (yes… “when” because they are real in my head) I meet Elisabeth, Silas, and Nathaniel:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528052763ra/25646699.gif" width="250" height="165" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Silas you precious</b> 😍🥰😍🥰<br><br><b>Nathaniel my love</b> 😍🥰😍🥰<br><br><b>Elisabeth my amazing boo</b> 😍🥰😍🥰<br><br>I love everything about this book!! It’s fast paced, has a good fantasy worthy (yes that’s a thing for me) plot, cracks me up, made me cry, had me invested in all of the main characters, was original, had a heroine that did not annoy me… AND IT IS A STANDALONE PEOPLE !!!!!!! I feel like a read a whole fantasy series.<br><br>the different versions of me while reading <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(in order) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1534181590ra/26122702.gif" width="175" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561649208ra/27734405.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561649121ra/27734402.gif" width="250" height="165" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Okay, okay, I gotta calm down for a bit… so this book is about Elisabeth, she’s a bit naive as she grew up isolated in a library (being in a library all day is a dream though)... And that's all I knew going in and that's all I think you should know as well haha :")<br><br>I thought the setting was going to be fully in a library and I really expected the world to be contained (especially because it is a standalone) but I was pleasantly surprised that the plot really goes beyond that. It’s another great example of blurbs not giving away too much, just enough to get readers interested.<br><br><b>If you have been following my updates you probably know that I CANNOT stop gushing about this book. I was practically posting an update of me freaking out almost every other chapter.</b> I didn’t want this book to end yet ;((<br><br><br><b>The dynamic between Elisabeth, Silas, and Nathaniel reminds me an awful lot of the dynamic between Tessa, Will, and Jem from TID… and I am not complaining</b> The plot is very different though but the vibe is a bit similar. Anyway, I LOVED their relationships and overall dynamic. This is <b>NOT A LOVE TRIANGLE</b> just to be clear… don’t worry that was not a spoiler. Their chemistry is just so well written and I was getting more invested as the story went on. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There was no plotting or scheming behind each others back and they were just a solid bunch and I really appreciated that. I’m tired of good people betraying each other! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>They had me so intrigued and <u>Nathaniel’s</u> “broody banter” had me laughing and giggling. Note: Nathaniel is bisexual and it wasn’t even a big deal. I really like it when fantasy have lgbtq characters and it it’s just normal for them because that’s how I feel like it should also be in our “normal” world. He felt so real to me and isn’t that the goal? ;)<br><br><u>Silas</u> was everything I wanted him to be and I fell in love with him. I don’t know how to describe him but hecc he’s amazing. He’s not one of those characters that are like plotting behind your back because, frankly, I’m tired of it. The epitome of Unconditional Love right there. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The thing with Silas is, he's not even human but he's the one that understands humanity the most and even though he isn't supposed to, he loves Nathaniel more than anything... I feel like there is so much to learn from him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I though I would get annoyed of <u>Elisabeth’s</u> naiveness but gladly I wasn’t. I thought that it was based on something and it made sense. I was able to relate to her greatly and she's amazing &lt;3<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Life is like the oil within a lamp. It can be measured, but the pace at which it burns depends on how the dail is turned day by day, how bright and fierce the flame. And there is no predicting whether the lamp might be knocked to the ground and shatter, when it could have blazed a lot longer. Such is the unpredictability of life.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Sorcery of Thorns</i> is now officially part of my best-standalones and has entered my favourites-of-all-time shelf because that is how much I loved it. It reminded me of how much I loved to read. I thought this was going to a “meh” read for me but, nope, I was wrong. <b>It was fun while still having the elements and emotional rollercoasters I want in a fantasy.</b> <br><br>This is a perfect fantasy standalone... that I <i>kind of</i> wish had a sequel but at the same time it's perfect the way it is. It did not fail to crack me up and tear me up.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You like this place?"<br>"Of course I do. It has books in it.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't think I have related to a quote more XD<br><br><b>
  <u>PLOT:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><b>
  <u>WRITING STYLE:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><b>
  <u>WORLD BUILDING:</u>
</b> ★★★★☆<br><b>
  <u>CHARACTERS:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><b>
  <u>THEMES:</u>
</b> ★★★★☆<br><b>
  <u>PACING:</u>
</b> ★★★★★ <br><b>
  <u>PAGE TURNER:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><br><a>instagram</a> | <a href="https://themoonwholistens.wixsite.com/mysite" rel="nofollow noopener"> blog</a> | <a>ko-fi</a> | <a>booksirens</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zM3c6bSaMFkmr8ljgMVXnSX3KqeoujYX0cf/sPhJMHyZC9XZlnOHT7pXP1uHal1k542fb7YRvrsQBMIPRgQtOA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JmwlTM+cuDsjJbV/YxYhLtq/lROoywJFFE7q32Mj4LNzqix87XUPLb/dQ0dkuSvXGMUg27ZgiunVjddg3W799w==')})
  }
